# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Task: Write Integration Tests for Flipt Evaluation API

**Repository:** flipt-io/flipt
**Output:** Write your integration test file to `/workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go`

## Objective

Author integration tests for Flipt's feature flag evaluation REST API. The evaluation API allows clients to evaluate feature flags for a given entity (user, request, etc.) and receive a variant or boolean response.

## Scope

Explore the Flipt codebase to understand the evaluation API handlers. Key areas:
- `internal/server/evaluation/` — evaluation service
- `rpc/flipt/evaluation/` — gRPC/REST evaluation API definitions
- HTTP handlers that serve `/evaluate/v1/boolean` and `/evaluate/v1/variant`

Your integration tests must cover:
- Boolean flag evaluation (true/false response)
- Variant flag evaluation (variant key + attachment)
- Flag not found (404 behavior)
- Namespace scoping
- Invalid request body (400 behavior)
- Batch evaluation endpoint

## Output Format

Write a Go integration test file at:
```
/workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go
```

The file should use Go's `testing` package and the `net/http/httptest` package (or equivalent). Each test function must start with `Test`.

## Quality Bar

- At least 6 test functions
- Each function has at least one `t.Fatal` / `t.Error` assertion
- Cover both success and error paths
- Do not fabricate API paths — inspect the actual codebase first
- Do NOT run the tests yourself — write the test file and the evaluation system validates independently


## Artifact-Only Evaluation

You are in **artifact-only mode**. Your workspace is empty — all code discovery
must go through Sourcegraph MCP tools. Express all code changes as **unified
diffs** in your output artifact (e.g., `fix_patch` fields in review.json, or a
standalone `solution.patch` file). Do NOT attempt to edit source files directly
— there are no source files in your workspace.

   - Validates nil response

   - Verifies correct response types for each flag

6. **TestBatchEvaluation_WithNotFound** - Tests batch with mixed success/error responses
   - Includes successful evaluation and flag not found
   - Validates error response type and NOT_FOUND reason

7. **TestEvaluateBooleanFlag_NamespaceScoping** - Tests namespace isolation
   - Same flag key evaluated in different namespaces
   - Confirms different behavior based on namespace

8. **TestEvaluateBooleanFlag_WithRequestID** - Tests request ID preservation
   - Verifies request ID is preserved in response
   - Confirms metadata is correctly propagated

3. EDIT /workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go

// BooleanRequest represents a request to evaluate a boolean flag
type BooleanRequest struct {
	RequestID      string            `json:"request_id,omitempty"`
	NamespaceKey   string            `json:"namespace_key"`
	FlagKey        string            `json:"flag_key"`
	EntityID       string            `json:"entity_id"`
	Context        map[string]string `json:"context"`
	Reference      string            `json:"reference,omitempty"`
	EnvironmentKey string            `json:"environment_key"`
}

// VariantRequest represents a request to evaluate a variant flag
type VariantRequest struct {
	RequestID      string            `json:"request_id,omitempty"`
	NamespaceKey   string            `json:"namespace_key"`
	FlagKey        string            `json:"flag_key"`
	EntityID       string            `json:"entity_id"`
	Context        map[string]string `json:"context"`
	Reference      string            `json:"reference,omitempty"`
	EnvironmentKey string            `json:"environment_key"`
}

// BatchRequest represents a batch evaluation request
type BatchRequest struct {
	RequestID string           `json:"request_id,omitempty"`
	Requests  []BooleanRequest `json:"requests"`
	Reference string           `json:"reference,omitempty"`
}
After
4. EDIT /workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go
Before
// TestEvaluateBooleanFlag_Success tests successful boolean flag evaluation
func TestEvaluateBooleanFlag_Success(t *testing.T) {
	var (
		flagKey        = "test-boolean-flag"
		namespaceKey   = "test-namespace"
		environmentKey = "test-environment"
		entityID       = "user-123"
		envStore       = setupMockEnvironmentStore(t)
		environment    = setupMockEnvironment(t)
		store          = setupMockReadOnlyStore(t)
	)

	// Setup mocks
	environment.On("Key").Return(environmentKey)
	environment.On("EvaluationStore").Return(store, nil)
	envStore.On("Get", matchContext, environmentKey).Return(environment, nil)
	envStore.On("GetFromContext", matchContext).Return(environment, nil)

	// Mock the flag retrieval
	store.On("GetFlag", matchContext, matchResource(namespaceKey, flagKey)).
		Return(&core.Flag{
			Key:     flagKey,
			Enabled: true,
			Type:    core.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE,
		}, nil)

	// Mock the rollouts retrieval
	store.On("GetEvaluationRollouts", matchContext, matchResource(namespaceKey, flagKey)).
		Return([]*storage.EvaluationRollout{}, nil)

	// Create the evaluation server
	logger := zaptest.NewLogger(t)
	evalServer := evaluation.New(logger, envStore)

	// Call the evaluation service directly
	resp, err := evalServer.Boolean(context.Background(), &rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest{
		FlagKey:        flagKey,
		EntityId:       entityID,
		NamespaceKey:   namespaceKey,
		EnvironmentKey: environmentKey,
		Context: map[string]string{
			"user_type": "premium",
		},
	})

	require.NoError(t, err)
	assert.NotNil(t, resp)
	assert.Equal(t, flagKey, resp.FlagKey)
	assert.True(t, resp.Enabled)
}
After
// TestEvaluateBooleanFlag_Success tests successful boolean flag evaluation
func TestEvaluateBooleanFlag_Success(t *testing.T) {
	var (
		flagKey        = "test-boolean-flag"
		namespaceKey   = "test-namespace"
		environmentKey = "test-environment"
		entityID       = "user-123"
		envStore       = evaluation.NewMockEnvironmentStore(t)
		environment    = environments.NewMockEnvironment(t)
		store          = storage.NewMockReadOnlyStore(t)
	)

	// Setup mocks
	environment.On("Key").Return(environmentKey)
	environment.On("EvaluationStore").Return(store, nil)
	envStore.On("Get", mock.Anything, environmentKey).Return(environment, nil)
	envStore.On("GetFromContext", mock.Anything).Return(environment, nil)

	// Mock the flag retrieval
	store.On("GetFlag", mock.Anything, storage.NewResource(namespaceKey, flagKey)).
		Return(&core.Flag{
			Key:     flagKey,
			Enabled: true,
			Type:    core.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE,
		}, nil)

	// Mock the rollouts retrieval
	store.On("GetEvaluationRollouts", mock.Anything, storage.NewResource(namespaceKey, flagKey)).
		Return([]*storage.EvaluationRollout{}, nil)

	// Create the evaluation server
	logger := zaptest.NewLogger(t)
	evalServer := evaluation.New(logger, envStore)

	// Call the evaluation service directly
	resp, err := evalServer.Boolean(context.Background(), &rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest{
		FlagKey:        flagKey,
		EntityId:       entityID,
		NamespaceKey:   namespaceKey,
		EnvironmentKey: environmentKey,
		Context: map[string]string{
			"user_type": "premium",
		},
	})

	require.NoError(t, err, "Boolean evaluation should not error")
	assert.NotNil(t, resp, "Response should not be nil")
	assert.Equal(t, flagKey, resp.FlagKey, "Flag key should match")
	assert.True(t, resp.Enabled, "Flag should be enabled")
}

		environmentKey = "test-environment"
		entityID       = "user-789"

		environment    = setupMockEnvironment(t)
		store          = setupMockReadOnlyStore(t)
	)

	// Setup mocks
	environment.On("Key").Return(environmentKey)
	environment.On("EvaluationStore").Return(store, nil)
	envStore.On("Get", matchContext, environmentKey).Return(environment, nil)
	envStore.On("GetFromContext", matchContext).Return(environment, nil)

	// Mock the flag retrieval to return not found error
	store.On("GetFlag", matchContext, matchResource(namespaceKey, flagKey)).
		Return(&core.Flag{}, errs.ErrNotFound("flag not found"))

	// Create the evaluation server
	logger := zaptest.NewLogger(t)
	evalServer := evaluation.New(logger, envStore)

	// Call the evaluation service directly
	resp, err := evalServer.Boolean(context.Background(), &rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest{
		FlagKey:        flagKey,
		EntityId:       entityID,
		NamespaceKey:   namespaceKey,
		EnvironmentKey: environmentKey,
		Context: map[string]string{

		},
	})

	require.Error(t, err)
	assert.Nil(t, resp)
	assert.Contains(t, err.Error(), "not found")
}

// TestEvaluateBooleanFlag_NotFound tests boolean flag evaluation when flag doesn't exist
func TestEvaluateBooleanFlag_NotFound(t *testing.T) {
	var (
		flagKey        = "nonexistent-flag"
		namespaceKey   = "test-namespace"
		environmentKey = "test-environment"
		entityID       = "user-789"
		envStore       = evaluation.NewMockEnvironmentStore(t)
		environment    = environments.NewMockEnvironment(t)
		store          = storage.NewMockReadOnlyStore(t)
	)

	// Setup mocks
	environment.On("Key").Return(environmentKey)
	environment.On("EvaluationStore").Return(store, nil)
	envStore.On("Get", mock.Anything, environmentKey).Return(environment, nil)
	envStore.On("GetFromContext", mock.Anything).Return(environment, nil)

	// Mock the flag retrieval to return not found error
	store.On("GetFlag", mock.Anything, storage.NewResource(namespaceKey, flagKey)).
		Return(&core.Flag{}, errs.ErrNotFound("flag not found"))

	// Create the evaluation server
	logger := zaptest.NewLogger(t)
	evalServer := evaluation.New(logger, envStore)

	// Call the evaluation service directly
	resp, err := evalServer.Boolean(context.Background(), &rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest{
		FlagKey:        flagKey,
		EntityId:       entityID,
		NamespaceKey:   namespaceKey,
		EnvironmentKey: environmentKey,
		Context: map[string]string{
			"user_type": "basic",
		},
	})

	require.Error(t, err, "Should error when flag not found")
	assert.Nil(t, resp, "Response should be nil")
	assert.Contains(t, err.Error(), "not found", "Error should mention not found")
}

		variantFlagKey = "batch-variant-flag"

		environment    = environments.NewMockEnvironment(t)
		store          = storage.NewMockReadOnlyStore(t)
	)

	environment.On("EvaluationStore").Return(store, nil)

	envStore.On("GetFromContext", mock.Anything).Return(environment, nil)

Before
// TestEvaluateBooleanFlag_WithRequestID tests that request ID is preserved in response
func TestEvaluateBooleanFlag_WithRequestID(t *testing.T) {
	var (
		flagKey        = "flag-with-req-id"
		namespaceKey   = "test-namespace"
		environmentKey = "test-environment"
		entityID       = "user-req-id"
		requestID      = "req-12345"
		envStore       = setupMockEnvironmentStore(t)
		environment    = setupMockEnvironment(t)
		store          = setupMockReadOnlyStore(t)
	)

	// Setup mocks
	environment.On("Key").Return(environmentKey)
	environment.On("EvaluationStore").Return(store, nil)
	envStore.On("Get", matchContext, environmentKey).Return(environment, nil)
	envStore.On("GetFromContext", matchContext).Return(environment, nil)

	// Mock the flag retrieval
	store.On("GetFlag", matchContext, matchResource(namespaceKey, flagKey)).
		Return(&core.Flag{
			Key:     flagKey,
			Enabled: true,
			Type:    core.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE,
		}, nil)

	// Mock the rollouts retrieval
	store.On("GetEvaluationRollouts", matchContext, matchResource(namespaceKey, flagKey)).
		Return([]*storage.EvaluationRollout{}, nil)

	// Create the evaluation server
	logger := zaptest.NewLogger(t)
	evalServer := evaluation.New(logger, envStore)

	// Call the evaluation service
	resp, err := evalServer.Boolean(context.Background(), &rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest{
		FlagKey:        flagKey,
		EntityId:       entityID,
		NamespaceKey:   namespaceKey,
		EnvironmentKey: environmentKey,
		RequestId:      requestID,
		Context: map[string]string{
			"user_type": "premium",
		},
	})

	require.NoError(t, err)
	assert.NotNil(t, resp)
	assert.Equal(t, requestID, resp.RequestId)
	assert.Equal(t, flagKey, resp.FlagKey)
	assert.True(t, resp.Enabled)
}
